Local Unset Kernel Term Sharing.

(** * Construction of affine lines

 We show that the propositional truncation of a ℤ-torsor, where ℤ
 is the additive group of the integers, behaves like an affine line.
 It's a contractible type, but maps from it to another type Y are determined
 by specifying where the points of T should go, and where the paths
 joining consecutive points of T should go. *)

(** ** Preliminaries *)

Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.
Require Import UniMath.MoreFoundations.Tactics.

Require Import UniMath.MoreFoundations.Univalence.

Require Import UniMath.MoreFoundations.PartA.
Require Import UniMath.MoreFoundations.Nat.
Require Import UniMath.Algebra.Monoids.
Require Import UniMath.Algebra.Groups.

(** ** Recursion for ℤ *)

Definition ℤRecursionData0 (P:ℤ->Type) (p0:P zero)
      (IH :∏ n, P(  toℤ n) -> P(  toℤ (S n)))
      (IH':∏ n, P(- toℤ n) -> P(- toℤ (S n))) := fun
          f:∏ i, P i =>
            (f zero = p0) ×
            (∏ n, f(  toℤ (S n)) = IH  n (f (  toℤ n))) ×
            (∏ n, f(- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))).

Definition ℤRecursionData (P:ℤ->Type)
      (IH :∏ n, P(  toℤ n) -> P(  toℤ (S n)))
      (IH':∏ n, P(- toℤ n) -> P(- toℤ (S n))) := fun
             f:∏ i, P i =>
               (∏ n, f(  toℤ (S n)) = IH  n (f (  toℤ n))) ×
               (∏ n, f(- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))).


P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))
IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
∃! y, ℤRecursionData0 (P:=P) p0 IH IH' y

P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))
IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
(∑ f : ∏ i : ℤ, P i,
 f zero = p0
 × (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
   × (∏ n : ℕ, f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))))
≃ (∑ f : ∏ w : ℕ ⨿ ℕ, P (negpos w),
   f (inr 0%nat) = p0
   × (∏ n : ℕ, f (inr (S n)) = IH n (f (inr n)))
     × f (inl 0%nat) = IH' 0%nat (f (inr 0%nat))
       × (∏ n : ℕ,
          f (inl (S n)) = IH' (S n) (f (inl n))))

P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))
IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
∏ x : ∏ y : ℤ, P y,

× (∏ n : ℕ, x (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (x (toℤ n)))
  × (∏ n : ℕ, x (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (x (- toℤ n)))
≃ weqonsecbase P negpos x (inr 0%nat) = p0
  × (∏ n : ℕ,
     weqonsecbase P negpos x (inr (S n)) =
     IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos x (inr n)))
    × weqonsecbase P negpos x (inl 0%nat) =
      IH' 0%nat (weqonsecbase P negpos x (inr 0%nat))
      × (∏ n : ℕ,
         weqonsecbase P negpos x (inl (S n)) =
         IH' (S n) (weqonsecbase P negpos x (inl n)))

P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))

       IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
      × weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
        IH' 0%nat
          (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
        × (∏ n : ℕ,
           weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
           IH' (S n) (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))),
(λ X : f zero = p0
       × (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
         × (∏ n : ℕ,
            f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))),
 (λ (h0 : f zero = p0)
  (pr2 : (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
         × (∏ n : ℕ,
            f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n)))),
  (λ (hp : ∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
   (hn : ∏ n : ℕ,
         f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))),
   h0,,
   hp,,
   hn 0%nat,,
   ((λ n : ℕ, hn (S n))
    :
    (λ _ : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
           IH' 0%nat
             (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat)),
     ∏ n : ℕ,
     weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
     IH' (S n) (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n)))
      (hn 0%nat))) (pr1 pr2) (Preamble.pr2 pr2))
   (pr1 X) (pr2 X))
  ((λ X : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat) = p0
          × (∏ n : ℕ,
             weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) =
             IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
            × weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
              IH' 0%nat
                (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
              × (∏ n : ℕ,
                 weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
                 IH' (S n)
                   (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))),
    (λ (h0 : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat) = p0)
     (pr2 : (∏ n : ℕ,
             weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) =
             IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
            × weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
              IH' 0%nat
                (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
              × (∏ n : ℕ,
                 weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
                 IH' (S n)
                   (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n)))),
     (λ (hp : ∏ n : ℕ,
              weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) =
              IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
      (pr3 : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
             IH' 0%nat
               (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
             × (∏ n : ℕ,
                weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
                IH' (S n)
                  (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n)))),
      (λ (h1' : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
                IH' 0%nat
                  (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat)))
       (hn : ∏ n : ℕ,
             weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
             IH' (S n)
               (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))),
       h0,,
       hp,,
       ((λ n : ℕ,
         match n as n0 return (...) with
         | 0%nat => h1'
         | S n0 => (λ ..., ...) n0
         end)
        :
        (λ _ : ∏ n : ℕ, f ... = IH n ...,
         ∏ n : ℕ, f (...) = IH' n (...)) hp))
        (pr1 pr3) (Preamble.pr2 pr3)) (pr1 pr2)
       (Preamble.pr2 pr2)) (pr1 X) (pr2 X)) y) = y

    
P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))
IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
f: ∏ y : ℤ, P y
∏
x : f zero = p0
    × (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
      × (∏ n : ℕ,
         f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))),
(λ X : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat) = p0
       × (∏ n : ℕ,
          weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) =
          IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
         × weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =

             (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
           × (∏ n : ℕ,
              weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
              IH' (S n)
                (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))),
 (λ (h0 : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat) = p0)
  (pr2 : (∏ n : ℕ,
          weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) =
          IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
         × weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
           IH' 0%nat
             (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
           × (∏ n : ℕ,
              weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
              IH' (S n)
                (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n)))),
  (λ (hp : ∏ n : ℕ,
           weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) =
           IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n)))
   (pr3 : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
          IH' 0%nat
            (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
          × (∏ n : ℕ,
             weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
             IH' (S n)
               (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n)))),
   (λ (h1' : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
             IH' 0%nat
               (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat)))
    (hn : ∏ n : ℕ,
          weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
          IH' (S n) (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))),
    h0,,
    hp,,
    ((λ n : ℕ,
      match n as n0 return (f ... = IH' n0 ...) with
      | 0%nat => h1'
      | S n0 => (λ n' : ℕ, hn n') n0
      end)
     :
     (λ _ : ∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ ...) = IH n (f ...),
      ∏ n : ℕ, f (- toℤ ...) = IH' n (f (...))) hp))
     (pr1 pr3) (Preamble.pr2 pr3)) (pr1 pr2)
    (Preamble.pr2 pr2)) (pr1 X) (pr2 X))
  ((λ X : f zero = p0
          × (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
            × (∏ n : ℕ,
               f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))),
    (λ (h0 : f zero = p0)
     (pr2 : (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
            × (∏ n : ℕ,

              f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
      (hn : ∏ n : ℕ,
            f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n))),
      h0,,
      hp,,
      hn 0%nat,,
      ((λ n : ℕ, hn (S n))
       :
       (λ _ : weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
              IH' 0%nat
                (weqonsecbase P negpos f (...)),

        weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (...)) =
        IH' (S n) (weqonsecbase P negpos f (...)))
         (hn 0%nat))) (pr1 pr2) (Preamble.pr2 pr2))
      (pr1 X) (pr2 X)) x) = x

                  (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat)))
       (hn : ∏ n : ℕ,
             weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
             IH' (S n)
               (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))),
       h0,,
       hp,,
       ((λ n : ℕ,
         match n as n0 return (...) with
         | 0%nat => h1'
         | S n0 => (λ ..., ...) n0
         end)
        :
        (λ _ : ∏ n : ℕ, f ... = IH n ...,
         ∏ n : ℕ, f (...) = IH' n (...)) hp))
        (pr1 pr3) (Preamble.pr2 pr3)) (pr1 pr2)
       (Preamble.pr2 pr2)) (pr1 X) (pr2 X)) y) = y

IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
f: ∏ y : ℤ, P y
h0: weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat) = p0
h1': ∏ n : ℕ,
weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr (S n)) = IH n (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr n))
hp: weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl 0%nat) =
IH' 0%nat (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inr 0%nat))
hn: ∏ n : ℕ,
weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl (S n)) =
IH' (S n) (weqonsecbase P negpos f (inl n))
h0,, h1',, hp,, (λ n : ℕ, hn n) = h0,, h1',, hp,, hn
 reflexivity. }

(λ X : ∑ y, ℤRecursionData0 (P:=P) p0 IH IH' y,
 (λ (f : ∏ i : ℤ, P i)
  (pr2 : ℤRecursionData0 (P:=P) p0 IH IH' f),
  (λ (h0 : f zero = p0)
   (h : (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
        × (∏ n : ℕ,
           f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n)))),
   (f,, h),, h0) (pr1 pr2) (Preamble.pr2 pr2)) (pr1 X)
   (pr2 X))
  ((λ X : hfiber
            (λ fh : ∑ y,
                    ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' y,
             pr1 fh zero) p0,
    (λ pr1 : ∑ y, ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' y,
     (λ (f : ∏ i : ℤ, P i)
      (h : ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' f)
      (h0 : Preamble.pr1 (f,, h) zero = p0),
      f,, h0,, h) (Preamble.pr1 pr1) (pr2 pr1))
      (pr1 X) (pr2 X)) y) = y

  
P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))
IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
∏
y : hfiber
      (λ fh : ∑ y, ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' y,
       pr1 fh zero) p0,
(λ X : ∑ y, ℤRecursionData0 (P:=P) p0 IH IH' y,
 (λ (f : ∏ i : ℤ, P i)
  (pr2 : ℤRecursionData0 (P:=P) p0 IH IH' f),
  (λ (h0 : f zero = p0)
   (h : (∏ n : ℕ, f (toℤ (S n)) = IH n (f (toℤ n)))
        × (∏ n : ℕ,
           f (- toℤ (S n)) = IH' n (f (- toℤ n)))),
   (f,, h),, h0) (pr1 pr2) (Preamble.pr2 pr2)) (pr1 X)
   (pr2 X))
  ((λ X : hfiber
            (λ fh : ∑ y,
                    ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' y,
             pr1 fh zero) p0,
    (λ pr1 : ∑ y, ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' y,
     (λ (f : ∏ i : ℤ, P i)
      (h : ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' f)
      (h0 : Preamble.pr1 (f,, h) zero = p0),
      f,, h0,, h) (Preamble.pr1 pr1) (pr2 pr1))
      (pr1 X) (pr2 X)) y) = y
 
P: ℤ → Type
p0: P zero
IH: ∏ n : ℕ, P (toℤ n) → P (toℤ (S n))
IH': ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) → P (- toℤ (S n))
f: ∏ i : ℤ, P i
h: ℤRecursionData (P:=P) IH IH' f
h0: pr1 (f,, h) zero = p0
(f,, h),, h0 = (f,, h),, h0
 reflexivity. }
Defined.


P: ℤ → Type

Defined.

(** ** Bidirectional recursion for ℤ *)

Definition ℤBiRecursionData (P:ℤ->Type) (IH :∏ i, P(i) -> P(1+i)) :=
  fun f:∏ i, P i => ∏ i, f(1+i)=IH i (f i).

l:= λ n : ℕ, weq_transportf P (k n): ∏ n : ℕ, P (one + toℤ n) ≃ P (toℤ (S n))
k': ∏ n : ℕ, - toℤ n = one + - toℤ (S n)

  (λ n : ℕ, ih' n): (∑ y,
 ℤRecursionData (P:=P) (λ n : ℕ, ih n)
   (λ n : ℕ, ih' n) y) ≃ P 0
f: ∏ i : ℤ, P i
n: ℕ
l n (IH (negpos (inr n)) (f (negpos (inr n)))) =
ih n (f (toℤ n))
 reflexivity. }

ih':= λ n : ℕ, (invweq (IH (- toℤ (S n))) ∘ l' n)%weq: ∏ n : ℕ, P (- toℤ n) ≃ P (- toℤ (S n))
G:= ℤRecursion_weq (P:=P) (λ n : ℕ, ih n)
  (λ n : ℕ, ih' n): (∑ y,
 ℤRecursionData (P:=P) (λ n : ℕ, ih n)

  (f (1 + natnattohz 0 (S n))) =

P: ℤ → Type
IH: ∏ i : ℤ, P i ≃ P (1 + i)
fh: ∑ y, ℤBiRecursionData (P:=P) (λ i : ℤ, IH i) y

P: ℤ → Type
IH: ∏ i : ℤ, P i ≃ P (1 + i)
fh: ∑ y, ℤBiRecursionData (P:=P) (λ i : ℤ, IH i) y
ℤBiRecursion_weq (P:=P) IH fh = pr1 fh 0

  reflexivity.             (* don't change the proof *)
Defined.

Definition ℤBiRecursion_inv_compute (P : ℤ → Type) (f : ∏ z : ℤ, P z ≃ P (1 + z)) (p : P 0) :
  pr1 (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p) 0 = p
  :=
    ! ℤBiRecursion_compute (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p)
      @
      homotweqinvweq (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p.

Definition ℤBiRecursion_transition_inv (P : ℤ → Type) (f : ∏ z : ℤ, P z ≃ P (1 + z)) (p : P 0) (z : ℤ) :
  pr1 (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p) (1 + z)
  =
  f z (pr1 (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p) z)
  :=
    pr2 (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p) z.

Definition ℤBiRecursion_transition_inv_reversed (P : ℤ → Type) (f : ∏ z : ℤ, P z ≃ P (1 + z)) (p : P 0) (z : ℤ) :
  pr1 (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p) z
  =
  invmap (f z) (pr1 (invmap (ℤBiRecursion_weq f) p) (1 + z))
  :=
    !homotinvweqweq _ _ @
     maponpaths (invmap (f z)) (! ℤBiRecursion_transition_inv f p z).

Notation "n + x" := (ac_mult _ n x) : action_scope.
Notation "n - m" := (quotient _ n m) : action_scope.
Local Open Scope action_scope.

(** ** Bidirectional recursion for ℤ-torsors *)

Definition GuidedSection {T:Torsor ℤ}
           (P:T->Type) (IH:∏ t, weq (P t) (P (one + t))) := fun
     f:∏ t, P t =>
       ∏ t, f (one + t) = IH t (f t).


T: Torsor ℤ
P: T → Type
IH: ∏ t : T, P t ≃ P (one + t)
t0: T
(∑ y, GuidedSection (P:=P) IH y) ≃ P t0

P: T → Type
IH: ∏ t : T, P t ≃ P (one + t)
t0: T
(∑ y, GuidedSection (P:=P) IH y) ≃ P t0

(** ** Guided null-homotopies from ℤ-torsors

 Let f be a map from a ℤ-torsor T to a type Y, and let s be a collection
 of target paths, connecting the images under f of consecutive points of T.

 A null-homotopy for f is a point y of Y, together with paths from
 y to each point in the image of f.  We say that it is "guided" by s
 if all the consecutive triangles commute.

 The main fact is that the type of guided null-homotopies for f is
 contractible.

 *)

Definition target_paths {Y} {T:Torsor ℤ} (f:T->Y) := ∏ t, f t=f(one + t).

Definition GHomotopy {Y} {T:Torsor ℤ} (f:T->Y) (s:target_paths f) := fun
        y:Y => ∑ h:nullHomotopyFrom f y, ∏ n, h(one + n) = h n @ s n.

Definition GuidedHomotopy {Y} {T:Torsor ℤ} (f:T->Y) (s:target_paths f) :=
  total2 (GHomotopy s).


Y: Type
T: Torsor ℤ
f: T → Y
s: target_paths f
t: T
GuidedHomotopy (f:=f) s → coconustot Y (f t)


Y: Type
T: Torsor ℤ
f: T → Y
s: target_paths f
t: T
GuidedHomotopy (f:=f) s → coconustot Y (f t)

  
Y: Type
T: Torsor ℤ
f: T → Y
s: target_paths f
t: T
y: Y
hp: GHomotopy (f:=f) s y
coconustot Y (f t)
 exact (y,,pr1 hp t).
Defined.

Definition GH_point {Y} {T:Torsor ℤ} {f:T->Y} {s:target_paths f}
           (yhp : GuidedHomotopy s) := pr1 yhp : Y.

Definition GH_homotopy {Y} {T:Torsor ℤ} {f:T->Y} {s:target_paths f}
           (yhp : GuidedHomotopy s)
     := pr1 (pr2 yhp)
     : nullHomotopyFrom f (GH_point yhp).

Definition GH_equations {Y} {T:Torsor ℤ} (f:T->Y) (s:target_paths f)
           (yhp : GuidedHomotopy s)
     := pr2 (pr2 yhp)
     : let h := GH_homotopy yhp in
       ∏ n, h(one + n) = h n @ s n.


Y: Type
T: Torsor ℤ
f: T → Y
s: target_paths f
iscontr (GuidedHomotopy (f:=f) s)

  (ℤTorsorRecursion_weq (P:=λ t : T, y = f t)
     (λ t : T, weq_pathscomp0r y (s t)) t0) h0 =
invweq
  (ℤTorsorRecursion_weq (P:=λ t : T, y = f t)
     (λ t : T, weq_pathscomp0r y (s t)) (one + t0))
  (h0 @ s t0)

  exact (ℤTorsorRecursion_transition_inv (λ t, weq_pathscomp0r y (s t)) _).
Defined.

  exact (b @ c @ a).

(** ** The image of the mere point in an affine line

 A torsor is nonempty, so it merely has a point, as does the
 corresponding affine line.  Here we name its image in Y. *)

Y

Y

Defined.
